***происходить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:происходить.html>происходи́ть</a> (453)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исходить.html>исходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">isxodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:происходить.html>происходи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proisxodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:произойти.html>произойти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take place, to happen, to occur</li>
<li>to derive, to be descended, to descend, to originate</li>
<li>to spring, to arise, to result, to take place</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:происшествие.html>происше́ствие</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">proisšéstvije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> согласовываться <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>частя́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>ре́чи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́го</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нского</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>рода</a>), 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***пройти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пройти.html>пройти́</a> (330)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-йти́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пройти.html>пройти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">projtí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проходить.html>проходи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pass, to go, to walk</li>
<li>to pass by</li>
<li><i>(time)</i> to pass, to go by, to elapse, to slip by
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пройти.html>прошло́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ли</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тюльпан.html>тюльпа́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зацвести.html>зацвёл</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:горшок.html>горшке́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne <b>prošló</b> i nedéli, kak tjulʹpán zacvjól v goršké.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">A tulip was blooming on a flowerpot in less than a week.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">A week didn't <b>pass</b>, but the tulip was blooming on a flowerpot.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пройти.html>пройдёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полгода.html>полго́да</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne <b>projdjót</b> i polgóda.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Not even half a year will pass.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be over</li>
<li><i>(meeting, gathering)</i> to go off, to be held</li>
<li>to study, to cover (in a course)</li></ol>

<p><b>прой<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ти.html>ти́</a></b>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проколоть.html>проколо́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prokolótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прокалывать.html>прока́лывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prokályvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проколоть.html>проколо́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pierce, to puncture, to prick, to perforate, to punch</li>
<li>to run a knife <i>(through)</i>, to stab</li></ol>

***прокатить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прокатить.html>прокати́ть</a> (21850)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катить.html>кати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прокатить.html>прокати́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prokatítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прока́тывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to roll (somewhere)</li>
<li>to entertain</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blackball, to vote against, to reject (a candidate at an election)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to criticize sharply and publicly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to quickly drive by/past</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ти́ть</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прокладывать.html>прокла́дывать</a> (12788)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кла́дывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-kládyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прокладывать.html>прокла́дывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prokládyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проложить.html>проложи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(a road, pipe etc.)</i> to build, to construct, to lay
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокладывать.html>прокла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:туннель.html>тунне́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokládyvatʹ</b> tunnɛ́lʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drive a tunnel</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to clear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокладывать.html>прокла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a> чему́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokládyvatʹ</b> dorógu čemú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pave the way for smth</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокладывать.html>прокла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokládyvatʹ</b> sebé dorógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to work/carve one's way; elbow one's way</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокладывать.html>прокла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokládyvatʹ</b> putʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make a path/road; break a trail</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокладывать.html>прокла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokládyvatʹ</b> nóvyje putí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to blaze new trails; pioneer</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to map
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокладывать.html>прокла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:курс.html>курс</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:судно.html>су́дна</a>, самолёта)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokládyvatʹ</b> kurs (súdna, samoljóta)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lay a course</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to interlay <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокладывать.html>прокла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лыми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лист.html>листа́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokládyvatʹ</b> knígu bélymi listámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to interleave a book</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прокладывать.html>прокла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:копирка.html>копи́рку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лист.html>листа́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokládyvatʹ</b> kopírku méždu listámi bumági</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to insert carbon paper between the sheets of paper</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***проклятие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проклятие.html>прокля́тие</a> (7987)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проклятие.html>прокля́тие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prokljátije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проклятие.html>прокля́тия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проклятие.html>прокля́тия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проклятие.html>прокля́тий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> damnation, condemnation, excommunication</li>
<li>anathema</li>
<li>curse, imprecation, malediction</li>
<li>extreme and imminent misfortune; continuous state of trouble</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анафема.html>ана́фема</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">anáfema</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проклятие.html>прокля́тие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prokljátije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>dammit!, damnation! (expressing strong negative emotions)</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>кля́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ти.html>ти</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>про-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-кля-</b>; суффикс: <b>-тиj</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-е</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:анафема.html>ана́фема</a></li>

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проклясть.html>прокля́сть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prokljástʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***проколоть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проколоть.html>проколо́ть</a> (21527)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колоть.html>коло́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проколоть.html>проколо́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prokolótʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прокалывать.html>прока́лывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pierce, to puncture, to prick, to perforate, to punch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проколоть.html>проколо́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́ши</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сережка.html>серёжек</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prokolótʹ</b> úši (dlja serjóžek)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">have one's ears pierced</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to run a knife <i>(through)</i>, to stab</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прокомментированный.html>прокомменти́рованный</a> (11883)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
